        <h2>
         <a href="/story/2011/11/19/1037990/-Police-Pepper-Spray-Passive-UC-Davis-Students" id="titleHref">
          Police Pepper Spray Passive UC Davis Students
         </a>
         <span style="white-space: nowrap">
         </span>
        </h2>
        <p class="author">
         <span>
          by
         </span>
         <a href="/user/OllieGarkey">
          OllieGarkey
         </a>
         <a alt="Follow this author" class="ajax type-user do-hotlist do-updateContent size-tiny off altTooltip" href="#?friend_id=280510&amp;is_stream=1">
          Follow
         </a>
         <span class="for">
          for
         </span>
         <a href="/blog/classwarfarenewsletter">
          ClassWarfare Newsletter: WallStreet VS Working Class Global Occupy movement
         </a>
        </p>
        <ul class="front-page-share clearfix">
         <li style="margin-left: 0px">
          <div class="fb-share-button" data-href="http://www.dailykos.com/story/2011/11/19/1037990/-Police-Pepper-Spray-Passive-UC-Davis-Students" data-layout="button_count">
          </div>
         </li>
         <li>
          <a class="twitter-share-button" data-count="horizontal" data-related="markos" data-text="Police Pepper Spray Passive UC Davis Students" data-url="http://www.dailykos.com/story/2011/11/19/1037990/-Police-Pepper-Spray-Passive-UC-Davis-Students" data-via="dailykos" href="https://twitter.com/share">
           Tweet
          </a>
         </li>
         <li>
          <a class="comments comment_count_with_new" data-comment_count="185" data-story_id="1037990" href="/story/2011/11/19/1037990/-Police-Pepper-Spray-Passive-UC-Davis-Students#comments">
           185 Comments
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </div>
       <div class="article-body">
        <div id="intro">
         <p>
          <iframe defang_allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="360" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/WmJmmnMkuEM?feature=player_embedded" width="640">
          </iframe>
         </p>
         <p>
          Earlier today, police at UC Davis broke up a group of students protesting the eviction of Occupy Davis. The occupiers sat and joined arms in protest of yesterday's eviction. They offered no resistance to police, and were not physically aggressive. Police pepper sprayed the protesters after they refused to move. Protesters chanted "Don't shoot students" and "Shame on you." After ten arrests were made, the police nervously retreated while students continued to chant "Whose University? Our university!".
         </p>
         <p>
          Last week, the SF Chronicle reported that after arrests at UC Berkeley, Captain Margo Bennet said that linking arms was "not nonviolent."
         </p>
         <p>
          There are multiple Youtube Videos showing the incident from several angles.
         </p>
         <p>
          The incident:
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wuWEx6Cfn-I">
           http://www.youtube.com/...
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=T3fIess2Vqs">
           http://www.youtube.com/...
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Police Retreat:
         </p>
         <p>
          <iframe defang_allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="360" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/oF72Es92T-U?feature=player_embedded" width="640">
          </iframe>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.WATO99.com">
           Crossposted
          </a>
          at WATO99.Com.
         </p>

         <div class="tooltipContents qtip-style-dk4_large qtip-pos-br">
          <p>
           <b>
            More Tagging tips:
           </b>
          </p>
          <p>
           A tag is a way to search for this diary. If someone is searching for "Barack Obama," is this a diary they'd be trying to find?
          </p>
          <p>
           Use a person's full name, without any title. Senator Obama may become President Obama, and Michelle Obama might run for office.
          </p>
          <p>
           If your diary covers an election or elected official, use election tags, which are generally the state abbreviation followed by the office. 
		CA-01 is the first district House seat. CA-Sen covers both senate races. NY-GOV covers the New York governor's race.
          </p>
          <p>
           Tags do not compound: that is, "education reform" is a completely different tag from "education". A tag like "reform" alone is probably not meaningful.
          </p>

          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Energy');return false;">

          </a>
          .
	If your diary is specific to a state, consider adding the state 
	(
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('California');return false;">
           California
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Texas');return false;">
           Texas
          </a>
          , etc).
	Keep in mind, though, that there are many wonderful and important diaries
	that don't fit in any of these tags. Don't worry if yours doesn't.
         </p>

             I have
             <em>
              never
             </em>
             seen that many cops in Davis in my
             <em>
              life
             </em>
             .
             <br/>
             And they found it necessary to bust out the pepper spray already?
             <br/>
             <em>
              Linking arms is now 'violence'???
             </em>
             Davis is the kind of town that has laws and ordinances giving bicycles the right of way over cars. You can't smoke a cigarette downtown, unless you are outside, walking, in one direction.
             <br/>
             We playfully call it, "The People's Republic of Davis".
            </p>
            <p>
             I can hear the cops discussing it beforehand in my head -
            </p>

             <strong>

             </strong>

             <em>
              totally
             </em>
             bring the
             <em>
              bear spray
             </em>
             . Those Marxists are asking for it if you get my
             <em>
              drift
             </em>
             ."
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>

             </strong>
             - "Yeah, everyone's doing it."
            </p>

             </strong>

             </em>
             here."

             The UC police departments aren't very large; for a 'tactical response' like this, they'll have a mutual aid agreement with the sheriff's office and local municipal departments.
            </p>
            <p>
             Both Yolo County deputies and Davis police officers wear blue uniforms, like the UC police officers.
            </p>

             <div class="ct">
              <p>
               Oh, they won't be charged with battery. That's true.
              </p>
              <p>
               But the CA trial bar will absolutely go after punitive damages on these cases. With these videos, I dont see any judges being willing to play gatekeeper on puni's.
              </p>
              <p>
               And puni's are not insurable.
              </p>
              <p>
               So the insurers will have to cough up more in defense costs, but settlements won't come so easy, especially if students and their parents want justice.
              </p>
              <p>
               Given that most of these students won't desperately need the money to get on with their lives ( like plaintiffs often do), they may be more willing to take these cases to trial.
              </p>
              <p>
               And I have a hard time seeing most reasonable jurors not being swayed by the first 30 seconds of the videos. Sometimes, there is evidence so bad, virtually every juror hates your client by the time they get done seeing it.Whom do you kick out off the jury? Students? Parents? Grandparents? Military? Virtually all would be offended.
              </p>
              <p>
               So, we'll see what happens....
              </p>

             <div class="ct">
              <blockquote>
               Don't they know that one of the requirements for employment as a cop is a complete absence of any sense of personal shame?
              </blockquote>
              How quickly everyone seems to forget the stories of the NYPD captain who helped insure that a protest went smoothly and efficiently, or the retired police captain who was arrested for protesting.
              <p>
               Branding all police officers as 'without shame' or, in a post in another thread, 'psychopaths' serves no one.
              </p>
              <p>
               There are bad cops out there who shouldn't have a badge let alone the right to use force, without question, and many of the decisions being made by both police commanders and their civilian bosses are deplorable and incredibly short-sighted. Labeling everyone who wears a badge is childish ranting, however.
              </p>

           <div class="cf">
            <p class="sig">
             Ordinary political process is dead. The Supreme Court killed it. In Chambers. With a gavel.
            </p>
            <p class="cb">
             by
             <a href="/user/uid:169447">
              Publius2008
             </a>
             on
             <a href="/comments/1037990/44000669#c80">
              Fri Nov 18, 2011 at 10:47:11 PM PST
             </a>
            </p>
            <p class="cl">
             [
             <a href="#c63">
              Parent
             </a>
             ]
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </li>
         <ul class="cm i1" id="k44000669">
          <li id="c82">
           <div class="cx" id="cx44000697">
            <h5>
             <a class="de">
             </a>
             <span class="cu">
              The letter the professor sent:
             </span>
             <span class="crd ntb">
              (
              <a href="/comments/1037990/44000697#c82?mode=alone;showrate=1#c82">
               16+ / 0-
              </a>
              )
             </span>
            </h5>
            <div class="crs">
             <dl>
              <dt>
               Recommended by:
              </dt>
              <dd>
               <a href="/user/uid:229952">
                We Won
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:224338">
                Cordyc
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:154702">
                mahakali overdrive
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:180257">
                ozsea1
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:25099">
                mauricehall
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:98722">
                aliasalias
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:99680">
                Orange County Liberal
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:17622">
                madhaus
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:171278">
                Floande
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:86112">
                pgm 01
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:86683">
                marykk
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:56317">
                jimreyn
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:17036">
                Creosote
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:96369">
                Matt Z
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:57293">
                lotlizard
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/user/uid:80060">
                kurt
               </a>
              </dd>
             </dl>
            </div>
            <div class="ct">
             <blockquote>
              I write to you and to my colleagues for three reasons:
              <p>
               1) to express my outrage at the police brutality which occurred against students engaged in peaceful protest on the UC Davis campus today
              </p>
              <p>
               2) to hold you accountable for this police brutality
              </p>
              <p>
               3) to demand your immediate resignation
              </p>
              <p>
               Today you ordered police onto our campus to clear student protesters from the quad. These were protesters who participated in a rally speaking out against tuition increases and police brutality on UC campuses on Tuesdaya rally that I organized, and which was endorsed by the Davis Faculty Association. These students attended that rally in response to a call for solidarity from students and faculty who were bludgeoned with batons,hospitalized, and arrested at UC Berkeley last week. In the highest tradition of non-violent civil disobedience, those protesters had linked arms and held their ground in defense of tents they set up beside Sproul Hall. In a gesture of solidarity with those students and faculty, and in solidarity with the national Occupy movement, students at UC Davis set up tents on the main quad. When you ordered police outfitted with riot helmets, brandishing batons and teargas guns to remove their tents today, those students sat down on the ground in a circle and linked arms to protect them.
              </p>
              <p>
               What happened next?
              </p>
              <p>
               Without any provocation whatsoever, other than the bodies of these students sitting where they were on the ground, with their arms linked, police pepper-sprayed students.Students remained on the ground, now writhing in pain, with their arms linked.
              </p>
              <p>
               What happened next?
              </p>
              <p>
               Police used batons to try to push the students apart. Those they could separate, they arrested, kneeling on their bodies and pushing their heads into the ground. Those they could not separate, they pepper-sprayed directly in the face, holding these students as they did so. When students covered their eyes with their clothing, police forced open their mouths and pepper-sprayed down their throats. Several of these students were hospitalized. Others are seriously injured. One of them, forty-five minutes after being pepper-sprayed down his throat, was still coughing up blood.
              </p>
              <p>
               This is what happened. You are responsible for it.
              </p>
              <p>
               You are responsible for it because this is what happens when UC Chancellors order police onto our campuses to disperse peaceful protesters through the use of force: students get hurt. Faculty get hurt. One of the most inspiring things (inspiring for those of us who care about students who assert their rights to free speech and peaceful assembly) about the demonstration in Berkeley on November 9 is that UC Berkeley faculty stood together with students, their arms linked together. Associate Professor of English Celeste Langan was grabbed by her hair, thrown on the ground, and arrested. Associate Professor Geoffrey OBrien was injured by baton blows. Professor Robert Hass, former Poet Laureate of the United States, National Book Award and Pulitzer Prize winner, was also struck with a baton. These faculty stood together with students in solidarity, and they too were beaten and arrested by the police. In writing this letter, I stand together with those faculty and with the students they supported.
              </p>
              <p>
               One week after this happened at UC Berkeley, you ordered police to clear tents from the quad at UC Davis. When students responded in the same waylinking arms and holding their groundpolice also responded in the same way: with violent force. The fact is: the administration of UC campuses systematically uses police brutality to terrorize students and faculty, to crush political dissent on our campuses, and to suppress free speech and peaceful assembly. Many people know this. Many more people are learning it very quickly.
              </p>
              <p>
               You are responsible for the police violence directed against students on the UC Davis quad on November 18, 2011. As I said, I am writing to hold you responsible and to demand your immediate resignation on these grounds.
              </p>
              <p>
               <strong>
                *
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p>
               I call for your resignation because you are unfit to do your job. You are unfit to ensure the safety of students at UC Davis. In fact: you are the primary threat to the safety of students at UC Davis. As such, I call upon you to resign immediately.
              </p>
             </blockquote>
            </div>
            <div class="cf">
             <p class="sig">
              Ordinary political process is dead. The Supreme Court killed it. In Chambers. With a gavel.
             </p>
             <p class="cb">
              by
              <a href="/user/uid:169447">
               Publius2008
              </a>
              on
              <a href="/comments/1037990/44000697#c82">
               Fri Nov 18, 2011 at 10:54:43 PM PST
              </a>
             </p>

              <a href="#c80">

              </a>

           <div class="ct">
            <blockquote>
             Police used batons to try to push the students apart. Those they could separate, they arrested, kneeling on their bodies and pushing their heads into the ground. Those they could not separate, they pepper-sprayed directly in the face, holding these students as they did so.
             <strong>
              When students covered their eyes with their clothing, police forced open their mouths and pepper-sprayed down their throats.
             </strong>
             Several of these students were hospitalized. Others are seriously injured. One of them, forty-five minutes after being pepper-sprayed down his throat, was still coughing up blood.
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             This is one powerful letter.

            </p>

          <div class="ct">
           <p>
            I spoke to the Davis chief of police and thought she was reasonable.
           </p>
           <p>
            And now I have seen the longer video on Huffington Post. The police were under absolutely no threat. They did this because they could.
           </p>
           <p>
            It could so easily have been avoided, with adult leadership.
           </p>
           <p>
            This is contemptible police work. These guys have been dressed (like the Village People), and armed, and trained, for war, probably courtesy of "Homeland Security." They have no idea how to deal patiently with peaceful student protests.
           </p>
           <p>
            The rules have to be different when peaceful protestors vastly outnumber the police. Peaceful, peaceful, peaceful. The police have to learn how to deal with peaceful protest. There's no place for this macho shit in America today. Middle-aged, middle-class people like me, it pisses us off to see kids hurt like this. It's shameful.
           </p>
           <p>
            And now, tomorrow, there will be thousands of protestors in Davis, and they will all be disgusted with the police. Good job, police. Nice work.
           </p>
           <p>
            Bad police--a small minority--have been the best source of new recruits to OWS. The violence of the few bad police sustains the OWS movement. This will be on the news tomorrow, nationally and internationally.
           </p>
           <p>
            I try to remember that these are the same people who would rush to protect us if we were in danger, but this was so utterly gratuitous.
           </p>
           <p>
            Don't you understand? We have cameras; the whole world really is watching. Want to arrest people? Arrest them. No need to torture them first.
           </p>
           <p>
            In the minds of the public, one act of obvious brutality wipes out thousands of hours of honorable police work. You must do better. This is America; you serve the American people. Police yourselves.
            <br/>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   if($.cookie('meter_user') !== 'false') {
		if ($('#ePostButton').length &gt; 0) {
		  $('#ePostButton').click(function() { 
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Posted Comment', { 
		      repliedTo: $(this).parents('#eP').prevAll('.cb').children('a').first().html() 
		    });
		  });
		}
		
		if (!!document.location.pathname.match('activate') &amp;&amp; $('h1:contains("Welcome to Daily Kos!")').length &gt; 0) {
		  DailyKos.Metrics.track('Signed Up');
		}
		
		if (document.location.pathname === '/') {
		  if (document.location.hostname.match(/^www|^dailykos/)) {
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Front Page');
		  } else {
		    var subdomain = document.location.hostname.split('.')[0];
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Vertical', { name: subdomain });
		  }
		}
		
		if ($('.ratinate').length &gt; 0) {
		  $('.ratinate').click(function() { DailyKos.Metrics.track('Recommended Comment') });
		}
		
		if ($('.do-addRating.type-story').length &gt; 0) {
		  $('.do-addRating.type-story').click(function() { DailyKos.Metrics.track('Recommended Story') });
		}
		
		if ($("form[action$='publishHow']").length &gt; 0) {
		  $(document).ready(function() {
			  $('.type-story.do-publishHow').click(function() { DailyKos.Metrics.track('Published Story') });
			 });
		}
		
		if (document.location.pathname.match(/^\/user/) &amp;&amp; $('li.here').length &gt; 0) {
		  if ($('.pageMenu:first li.here').children('a').html().match(/Stream/)) {
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Stream', { name: $('.name').children('a').html() });
		  } else if ($('.pageMenu:first li.here').children('a').html().match(/Profile/)) {
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Profile', { name: $('.name').children('a').html() });
		  } else if ($('.pageMenu:last li.here').children('a').html().match(/My Recent Replies/)) {
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Replies');
		  }
		} 
		
		if ($('#search-tabbed').length &gt; 0) {
		  DailyKos.Metrics.track('Searched');
		}
		
		if ($('#group-tables').length &gt; 0) {
			DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Groups List');
		}
		
		if (document.location.pathname.match(/^\/groups/) &amp;&amp; $("#group_info").length &gt; 0) {
		  DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Group', { name: $('.name').children('a').text() });
		}
		
		if ($('.do-hotlist.type-user, .do-unHotlist.type-user').length &gt; 0) {
		  $('.do-hotlist.type-user, .do-unHotlist.type-user').click(function() {
		    var nickName;
		    nickName = ($(this).prev('a').html() || $('.name a').html())
		    if ($(this).hasClass('do-hotlist')) {
		      DailyKos.Metrics.track('Followed User', { nickname: nickName }) 
		    } else if ($(this).hasClass('do-unHotlist')) {
		      DailyKos.Metrics.track('Unfollowed User', { nickname: nickName }) 
		    }    
		  });
		}
	}
  </script>
